<p style="text-align: justify;"><strong><span style="font-family: book antiqua,palatino; font-size: 12pt; color: #3366ff;"><span style="line-height: 115%;"><span style="color: #0000ff;">Baba Times Digest | 20 April 2014 18:56 EST | New York Edition</span></span></span><span style="color: #3366ff;"><span style="line-height: 115%;"><span style="color: #0000ff;"></span></span></span><span style="color: #3366ff;"><span style="line-height: 115%;"><br /></span></span></strong></p>

<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: center;" align="center"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">Everything Is Yoga</b></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: center;" align="center"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">Divine Life Society Publication: - </b><a href="http://www.dlshq.org/messages/everythingyoga.htm"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">Everything Is Yoga</b></a><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"> by Swami Chidananda</b></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;">Worshipful homage to that supreme, eternal, universal Being, Lord Krishna, who revealed Himself in and through the Gita wisdom teachings that He imparted for all mankind, for all times, through His beloved devotee and disciple, Arjuna. He not only revealed His divine nature through His Bhagavad Gita teachings, He also revealed how man can realize Him fully, can experience Him, and, ultimately, how man can merge himself in Him to become one with Him. All this He taught within the compass of 700 brief verses contained in 18 chapters.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">Main teaching</b></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;">Attain through Yoga the supreme human experience of our essential non-differentiation from Him; the experience that liberates us forever from all sorrow, all confusion and delusion; the experience that liberates us once and for all from a return to successive birth, death and rebirth in this mortal world. </span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;">The four classical <i>yogas </i>arechannelizing our action potential through <i>karma</i> <i>yoga</i> for God-realization, channelizing our sentiment and emotion potential for realizing God through <i>bhakti</i> <i>yoga</i>, channelizing our minds power of concentration for attaining God-realization through <i>raja</i> <i>yoga</i>, through meditation, and channelizing our intellectual potential of analysis, logic, discrimination and reasoning to attain illumination through <i>jnana</i> <i>yoga</i>. H<a name="_GoBack"></a>ere in the Gita we have 18 <i>yogas</i>. Everything is <i>yoga</i>. He covers the whole of human life in His teaching.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">Everything is <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">yoga</i></b></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;">The central teaching is that, in fact, all life is <i>yoga</i>. Life is to be lived as the great <i>sadhana</i>, the great <i>yoga</i>. All actions constitute <i>yoga</i>. Everything that you think is <i>yoga</i>. Everything that you speak is <i>yoga</i>. Everything that you do is <i>yoga</i>. Life is the supreme <i>yoga</i>, every part of it. </span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;">Each and every one of our actions from morning till evening should have a Godward thrust; they are to be engaged in for attaining illumination. Everything in our life is and ought to be enlightenment oriented. Breathing, sitting, standing, running, resting, working, lying, waking, dreaming, sleeping, all constitute that one single process<i>yoga</i>. So there are not merely 18 <i>yogas</i>. There are innumerable <i>yogas</i> every moment. This is the great truth about you, about each and every one of us.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;">May the grace of the Supreme and the benedictions of revered and beloved Holy Master Gurudev Swami Sivanandaji enable us to fully recognize this truth, fully assimilate this truth, fully live in the light of this truth, and thus become the Truth. May God bless us all! </span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;" class="MsoHyperlink"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">Excerpts from:</b></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;"><a href="http://www.dlshq.org/messages/everythingyoga.htm"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">Everything Is Yoga</b></a><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"> by Swami Chidananda</b></span><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;"> </span></p>
